<!DOCTYPE HTML PUBLIC "-//W3C//DTD HTML 4.0 Transitional//EN"><html lang="en-US"><head><title>EdgarFiling</title><meta content="text/html; charset=windows-1252" ><meta name="GENERATOR" content="MSHTML 8.00.7601.18094" ></head><body bgcolor="#ffffff"><p style="text-align: right;"><strong>EXHIBIT 99.1</strong></p><p style="text-align: center;"><font style="font-size: 14pt;"><strong>MiNK Therapeutics Reports Corporate Update and Third Quarter 2022 Financial Results</strong></font></p><p style="text-align: center;"><strong></strong></p><p>
   <p align="left"><em>-&#160; Five presentations on clinical data and novel pipeline candidates at the Society of Cancer Immunotherapy (SITC) Meeting<br ></em><em>-&#160; R&amp;D Day on November 10, 2022, from 4:00-6:00pm ET in Boston and via webcast</em></p>    <p>NEW YORK, Nov.  03, 2022  (GLOBE NEWSWIRE) -- MiNK Therapeutics, Inc., a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company pioneering the discovery, development, and commercialization of allogeneic, off-the-shelf, invariant natural killer T (iNKT) cell therapies to treat cancer and other immune-mediated diseases, today reported financial results for the third quarter 2022 and provided a corporate update.</p>    <p>&#8220;Our team has continued to excel as we focus on advancing both our clinical stage programs and next-generation pipeline, while scaling up our internal cGMP manufacturing capabilities,&#8221; said Jennifer Buell, President and CEO, of MiNK. &#8220;This progress is exemplified in the five upcoming presentations at this year&#8217;s SITC conference and our upcoming R&amp;D Day.&#8221;</p>    <p><strong>Business Progress and Upcoming Milestones:</strong></p>    <p>Five abstracts accepted for presentation at Society of Cancer Immunotherapy 37<sup>th</sup> Annual Meeting, November 8<sup>th</sup> to 12<sup>th</sup>:</p>    <ul type="disc"><li>Clinical data from agenT-797 (allo-iNKTs) alone or in combination with anti-PD-1 in advanced solid tumor cancers, severe viral ARDS, and relapsed/refractory multiple myeloma.</li><li>Data on our new therapeutic candidates, MiNK-215, a novel FAP-CAR-iNKT, and MiNK-413, a differentiated allogeneic armored-BCMA-CAR-iNKT.</li><li>First reports of novel mechanisms of agenT-797, improving effector functions within the tumor microenvironment.<br ></li></ul>    <p>MiNK to host R&amp;D Day on November 10<sup>th</sup>, 2022, from 4:00 &#8211; 6:00pm ET:</p>    <ul type="disc"><li>Leaders in cancer and immunology will discuss new clinical data, novel iNKT mechanisms of action, R&amp;D strategy, and internal scalable cell manufacturing.</li><li>Featured speakers include members of management and:  <ul type="circle"><li>Manuel Hidalgo, M.D, Ph.D., <em>Chief of the Division of Hematology and Medical Oncology at Weill Cornell Department of Medicine.</em></li><li>Terese Hammond, M.D., <em>Program Medical Director, Providence Saint John&#8217;s Health Center; Director, SCoRE (Sound Center of Research Excellence).</em></li><li>Lydia Lynch, Ph.D., <em>Leader of the Harvard Lynch Lab and Associate Professor of Medicine, Brigham and Women's Hospital, Harvard Medical School.</em></li><li>David Einstein, M.D., <em>Genitourinary Oncologist, Beth Israel Deaconess Medical Center; Assistant Professor, Harvard Medical School.</em></li><li>Mark Exley, Ph.D., <em>Expert in iNKT biology and Scientific Advisor to MiNK and CSO of Imvax.</em></li></ul>  </li><li>The event will be live webcasted and institutional investors and analysts are invited to attend in person. Individuals interested in attending the event in-person should contact MiNK Therapeutics Investor Relations at investor@minktherapeutics.com. To register for the webcast, please click here.</li></ul>    <p><strong>Fourth Quarter and Full Year 2021 Financial Results</strong></p>    <p>We ended the third quarter 2022 with a cash balance of&#160;$24.2 million as compared to $38.9 million&#160;at&#160;December 31, 2021. Cash used in operations for the nine-months and third quarter ended&#160;September 30, 2022, was $14.4 million, and $5.6 million respectively, compared to $11.1 million and $3.5 million for the same periods in 2021. The increased funding was related to the internalization of our cGMP manufacturing of agent-797 for clinical trial supply.</p>    <p>Net loss for the quarter ended&#160;September 30, 2022, was&#160;$6.3 million or $0.19 per share, compared to a net loss for the same period of 2021 of&#160;$14.3 million or $0.59 per share. Net loss for the nine months ended September 30, 2022, was $20.2 million, or $0.60 per share compared to $24.4 million and $1.01 per share for the nine months ended September 30, 2021.</p>    <p><br > <br ></p>  <table style="width:100%; border-collapse:collapse !important;;border-collapse: collapse; "><tr><td colspan="9" style="padding-left: 0 ; padding-right: 0 ; text-align: center ;  vertical-align: middle; "><strong>Summary Consolidated Financial Information</strong></td><td colspan="3" style="padding-left: 0 ;
